NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

[Part VI—Sec. 4

PUBLIC NOTICE
C-Kam Steel Wire Solutions Private Limited.
Regd. Off: Ceebros Centre, III Floor, 39-40, Montieth Road, Egmore, Chennai-600 008.
Pursuant to Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, notice is hereby given that at the Extraordinary General Meeting
of the Company held on 15th June 2015, the following Special Resolutions were passed unanimously to Voluntarily
wind up the Company.
RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the applicable provisions of the Companies Act, 2013/ Companies’ Act, 1956, the consent
of the members of the Company be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the Company as the members’ voluntary
winding up, w. e. f. June 15, 2015
RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the applicable provisions of the Companies Act, 2013/Companies’ Act, 1956,
Shri P Sitaraman, Fellow Chartered Accountant (Membership No. 028541) be and is hereby appointed as ‘the Liquidator’
of the Company for the purpose of the members’ voluntary winding up of the affairs of the Company.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT the consent of the members of the Company be and is hereby accorded to sanction the
remuneration of liquidator of (Rs.1,00,000/- Rupees One Lac) in addition to the actual out of pocket expenses for the
winding up of the affairs of the Company.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT Shri P Sitaraman, Liquidator be and is hereby authorized to exercise all the powers
as per the applicable provisions of the Companies Act, 2013/Companies’ Act, 1956 to effectively winding up the affairs of
the Company.

Madurai,
3rd July 2015.

C-Kam Steel Wire Solutions Private Limited,
RAMALINGAM MURALI,
Chairman.

Form No. 151
[See rule 315]
